## 2026-04-09 Research Report

### New Topic Recommendations

1. **程式設計師笑話 / Programmer Jokes** (slug: `programmer-jokes`, category: Humor)
   - Very strong niche community in Taiwan; evergreen content on PTT joke board, Dcard funny board, TechOrange, INSIDE
   - Classic format: logic/literal thinking jokes (the "5 apples" joke is iconic and universally recognized among tech workers)
   - High shareability in LINE group chats among office workers and students
   - SEO targets: 工程師笑話, 程式設計師笑話, IT笑話, 工程師語錄
   - Content pool: large — logic jokes, bug/debugging jokes, programmer stereotypes, tech puns

2. **星座語錄 / Zodiac Quotes** (slug: `zodiac-quotes`, category: Social)
   - Consistently high search volume year-round, peaks around new year and Valentine's
   - 2026 content hook: annual horoscope predictions driving fresh searches ("2026星座運勢")
   - Especially popular among female users 18–35; strong on LINE Today, Marie Claire TW
   - Sub-formats: zodiac personality traits, dating compatibility lines, zodiac "幹話"
   - SEO targets: 星座語錄, 12星座, 星座特質, 星座情話

3. **幹話語錄 / Sarcastic/Absurd Quotes** (slug: `witty-comebacks`, category: Humor)
   - Z-generation internet culture trend: "活人感", "低山臭水遇知音", "情緒價值" all trending in 2025–2026
   - High engagement on Dcard and PTT among 18–25 demographic
   - Format: short, punchy, self-deprecating or absurdist one-liners
   - Differentiated from cold-jokes by tone (sardonic vs. punny)
   - SEO targets: 幹話語錄, 搞笑語錄, 金句, 廢話文學

4. **勵志語錄 / Motivational Quotes** (slug: `motivational-quotes`, category: Motivation)
   - Evergreen, broad appeal across all demographics
   - High search volume ("語錄 2026", "激勵語錄", "正能量語錄")
   - Works well for back-to-school season (Sept), year-end (Dec), New Year (Jan)
   - Differentiator: FunTextHub should focus on "輕勵志" (light motivation) — witty and relatable, not preachy
   - SEO targets: 勵志語錄, 正能量語錄, 人生金句, 激勵短句

### Content Trends

- **愚人節笑話 (April Fools' — IMMEDIATE OPPORTUNITY)**: April 1 just passed; content remains highly searched through mid-April. Taiwanese brands had viral April Fools' campaigns (清心, 爭鮮). Adding a seasonal "愚人節笑話" collection or tagging existing cold-jokes with April Fools' could capture residual traffic.
- **Gen Z Internet Slang Integration**: Terms like "活人感", "破防", "情緒價值", "低山臭水遇知音" are trending. Using these naturally in editorNotes and tags would improve content relevance for younger audiences.
- **母親節 (Mother's Day — May 10, 2026)**: Exactly 1 month away. A "搞笑媽媽語錄" or sweet quotes targeting mom/family themes would have high seasonal search traffic in late April through mid-May.
- **職場主題**: Office humor consistently popular; "公司笑話" had notable mentions around April Fools'. Programmer jokes and workplace quotes should be bundled.

### Existing Topic Updates

- **cold-jokes (冷笑話)**: Add more **諧音梗** (homophone puns) — search results show these are the most shared format in 2026. Classic structure: "什麼X最Y？Z，因為..." 
- **sweet-quotes (暖男語錄)**: Add **母親節** themed variations before May 10; also consider "給媽媽的情話" sub-theme.
- **cheesy-pickups (土味情話)**: Tech-themed pickup lines trending ("Are you Wi-Fi? Because I'm feeling a connection") — add bilingual tech/programmer pickup lines as a sub-theme; strong crossover with programmer-jokes audience.

### Action Priority (Suggested Order)
1. Create `programmer-jokes` topic (high demand, clear content pool)
2. Create `motivational-quotes` topic (broad evergreen appeal)
3. Add Mother's Day variations to `sweet-quotes` before May 10
4. Create `zodiac-quotes` topic (consistent search volume)
5. Create `witty-comebacks` / 幹話語錄 topic (Z-gen trend)

## 2026-04-10 Research Report

### Status Update
- `programmer-jokes` topic has been created (confirmed in src/content/topics/)
- Remaining from yesterday's priority list: motivational-quotes, Mother's Day sweet-quotes update, zodiac-quotes, witty-comebacks

### New Topic Recommendations

1. **職場語錄 / Workplace Quotes** (slug: `workplace-quotes`, category: Lifestyle)
   - Consistently high demand on 518.com.tw, FashionGuide, and PTT workplace boards
   - "工作不會害你，只有人才會" style content resonates broadly; office humor is evergreen
   - Strong LINE group sharing culture among 25–45 office workers
   - Sub-formats: satirical workplace observations, boss/colleague dynamics, resignation fantasy quotes, hustle culture backlash
   - SEO targets: 職場語錄, 上班族語錄, 辦公室笑話, 職場幽默, 工作金句
   - Differentiator from programmer-jokes: broader audience (all industries), focuses on emotions and relationships, not just logic humor

2. **廢話文學 / Absurdist Nonsense Literature** (slug: `absurd-wisdom`, category: Humor)
   - Major 2025–2026 Z-gen trend on Dcard and social media; "廢話文學" format involves stating the obvious in a profound-sounding way
   - Example format: "沒有傘的人，就算跑得再快，也會被雨淋濕" — sounds philosophical, is completely obvious
   - Extremely high shareability; low content creation barrier
   - Overlaps with "幹話" (sarcastic absurdism) but has a distinct deadpan-profound tone
   - SEO targets: 廢話文學, 廢文語錄, 搞笑語錄, 哲學廢話, 廢話金句
   - Source pool: endless — any obvious statement reframed as wisdom

3. **台劇語錄 / Taiwanese Drama Quotes** (slug: `drama-quotes`, category: Romance)
   - Dedicated Instagram account @twdramaquotes confirms sustained audience interest
   - Taiwanese dramas on Netflix (愛情白皮書, 不夠善良的我們) driving 2025–2026 interest
   - Strong crossover with sweet-quotes audience; many drama lines work as romantic/emotional quotes
   - Bilingual potential: fans often search for English subtitles of iconic lines
   - SEO targets: 台劇語錄, 台劇經典台詞, 台劇金句, 偶像劇語錄
   - Content differentiation: focus on timeless emotional resonance, not spoiler-heavy plot references

4. **地獄笑話 / Dark Humor Jokes** (slug: `dark-humor`, category: Humor)
   - Multiple 2026 blog aggregators (pixnet, arielhsu.tw) explicitly label content "地獄笑話" — showing active search demand
   - Distinct from cold-jokes (冷笑話): darker, edgier, more shock-based humor
   - Very popular among 18–30 male audience on PTT; increasingly mainstream
   - Requires careful curation — must remain clean enough for broad audiences (no offensive targets)
   - SEO targets: 地獄笑話, 黑色幽默笑話, 大人笑話, 無厘頭笑話
   - Risk: requires stricter content moderation; recommend starting with 10–15 well-curated items

### Content Trends

- **2026 台灣 Z-gen Slang Integration**: Key terms to embed naturally in editorNotes and tags: 「破防」(emotionally struck), 「本斛但大」(tempted and gave in), 「好99」(exaggerated cute/approval), 「甘阿捏」(classic Taiwanese: "is that so?"), 「真冰涼」(viral catchphrase). Using these in tags improves discovery among younger audiences browsing social media.
- **母親節 (May 10, 2026) — 30 days out**: High-urgency seasonal window. Sweet-quotes should add 母親節 variations by late April. Potential sub-theme: "給媽媽的土味情話" crossover between cheesy-pickups and Mother's Day that would stand out.
- **TikTok Global Trends Crossover**: "God Forbid" witty-comeback format and self-aware humor ("I was not built for discomfort") map directly onto the witty-comebacks / 幹話語錄 topic. International trend validates the topic's timing.
- **地獄梗圖 Search Spike**: Multiple 2026 blog posts and meme sites feature explicit "地獄笑話" labeling — indicates active category search, not just incidental tagging.
- **Workplace Frustration Content**: Office humor memes on TikTok (#辦公室搞笑 hashtag active) and satirical workplace quotes on 518.com.tw confirm sustained demand in this category.

### Existing Topic Updates

- **programmer-jokes** (newly created): Ensure bilingual tech pickup line crossover content is tagged for cheesy-pickups discovery. Consider "工程師語錄" variations that overlap with workplace-quotes territory.
- **sweet-quotes (暖男語錄)**: PRIORITY — add 母親節 themed items before May 10. Suggested angle: tender messages from adult children to mothers (vs. romantic focus of current items). Also consider "給自己的情話" (self-love quotes) — trending on Dcard women's board.
- **cheesy-pickups (土味情話)**: Add **廢話文學**-style pickup lines: "你知道嗎，沒有你陪我的夜晚，月亮還是會升起來，但我就是不開心" — obvious-yet-sincere format is trending and fits the cheesy pickup style.
- **cold-jokes (冷笑話)**: Explore **地獄笑話** adjacent content — jokes with unexpected dark twists that are absurd rather than mean. Could be tagged separately if dark-humor topic is created.

### Updated Action Priority

1. ~~Create `programmer-jokes` topic~~ ✅ Done
2. Add Mother's Day variations to `sweet-quotes` (deadline: before May 10)
3. Create `motivational-quotes` topic (broad evergreen appeal)
4. Create `workplace-quotes` topic (strong sustained demand, broad audience)
5. Create `witty-comebacks` / 幹話語錄 + `absurd-wisdom` / 廢話文學 (Z-gen trend, high shareability)
6. Create `zodiac-quotes` topic (consistent search volume)
7. Evaluate `drama-quotes` and `dark-humor` topics for future batch

### New Topic Recommendations

1. **廢話文學 / Absurd Wisdom** (slug: `absurd-wisdom`, category: Humor)
   - Confirmed still highly active on Dcard in 2026 — dedicated threads with recent posts (Jan 2026 entries spotted)
   - Signature format examples verified: "在非洲，每六十秒，就有一分鐘過去"; "每呼吸60秒，就減少一分鐘的壽命"; "誰能想的到，這名16歲少女，在四年前，只是一名12歲少女"
   - Format is extremely easy to consume and share; works perfectly as short posts on LINE, IG Stories, Threads
   - SEO targets: 廢話文學, 廢話語錄, 廢話金句, 哲學廢話, 搞笑語錄
   - **Recommendation: Create immediately — low content risk, high viral potential, Dcard audience confirmed**

2. **勵志語錄 / Motivational Quotes** (slug: `motivational-quotes`, category: Motivation)
   - Multiple high-authority Taiwan sites confirmed active curation: Ariel Hsu (arielhsu.tw), CyberLink Blog, 經理人, 商周財富網, ProjectManager.com.tw
   - Content themes confirmed: 追夢 (chasing dreams), 勇氣 (courage), 重生 (rebirth), 自我 (self-identity) — map directly to FunTextHub categories
   - FunTextHub differentiator: focus on "輕勵志" — witty, relatable, non-preachy; under 30 characters preferred
   - SEO targets: 勵志語錄, 正能量語錄, 激勵短句, 座右銘, 每日一句, 心靈語錄
   - Search demand confirmed evergreen; peaks January, September (school year starts), year-end
   - **Recommendation: Create next after absurd-wisdom**

3. **節日笑話 / Seasonal Holiday Jokes** (slug: `holiday-jokes`, category: Humor)
   - Easter 2026 joke content actively circulating on Pinterest (68 ideas board confirmed), Reddit, Parade, RD.com
   - Format: clean pun-based jokes ("Why are Easter eggs funny? They're full of yolks")
   - Taiwan angle: 清明節 (April 4, just passed), 端午節 (June 2), 中秋節 (September) — Taiwan holiday cycle offers recurring seasonal hooks
   - Bilingual opportunity strong — same jokes localized for zh-tw and en audiences
   - SEO targets: 清明笑話, 端午笑話, 節日笑話, Easter jokes, holiday jokes
   - Risk: seasonal content has traffic spikes but quieter off-season periods; tag carefully by holiday
   - **Recommendation: Plan for 端午節 (June 2) content now; consider adding "seasonal" tag to existing cold-jokes for discoverability**

4. **職場語錄 / Workplace Quotes** (slug: `workplace-quotes`, category: Lifestyle)
   - Continued confirmation from Dcard popular board and 518.com.tw; office humor consistently among top shared LINE content for 25–45 demographic
   - Strong crossover with programmer-jokes audience; "辦公室幽默" and "老闆語錄" are high-volume searches
   - SEO targets: 職場語錄, 上班族語錄, 辦公室笑話, 工作金句
   - **Recommendation: Develop in parallel with motivational-quotes (different category/audience)**

### Content Trends

- **廢話文學 Momentum Confirmed**: Dcard posts from Jan 2026 still using this format confirms it hasn't peaked — timing for FunTextHub entry is good.
- **母親節 (May 10) — URGENT**: 29 days away. Research found multiple 2026-labeled 母親節語錄 resources already ranking well. Content angles: (a) 搞笑版 — "謝謝你沒把我退貨"; (b) 感人版 — "妳養我長大，我陪妳變老"; (c) 土味情話版 — "媽，你就是我人生的Wi-Fi，怎麼離開你都沒有訊號". The third angle uniquely crosslinks cheesy-pickups with sweet-quotes audience.
- **Easter/Spring Jokes**: Easter 2026 content is actively circulating in English-language social media (Pinterest, Reddit, Instagram). These clean pun-based jokes ("Egg-cited", "Hoppy Easter") work well for FunTextHub's English content and could attract international traffic. Plan 清明/端午 Chinese equivalents.
- **Dad Jokes / 爸爸笑話**: Multiple 2026 trending joke compilations explicitly label content "dad jokes" — confirmed cross-cultural appeal. Research showed 376+ jokes trending on Reddit pun humor formats. FunTextHub's cold-jokes topic overlaps heavily; consider adding "爸爸笑話" as a tag to existing cold-jokes items.
- **幹話語錄 Dcard Activity**: Dedicated 幹話 topic confirmed on Dcard with ongoing posts — audience exists and is engaged. Overlaps with witty-comebacks concept from previous research.

### Existing Topic Updates

- **sweet-quotes (暖男語錄)** — **URGENT**: Add 母親節 themed items within 2 weeks. Suggested new items: (1) 搞笑感恩句; (2) 成年子女視角的感動句; (3) "給媽媽的土味情話" crossover items. Research confirms 2026 searches are active for 母親節語錄 幽默/搞笑.
- **cold-jokes (冷笑話)**: Add "爸爸笑話" and "諧音梗" tags to existing items to capture dad-jokes search traffic. New content angle: Easter/清明 seasonal pun jokes bilingual.
- **programmer-jokes**: Add "工程師語錄" and "職場" tags to improve discoverability for users searching workplace humor. Consider "軟體工程師vs現實" format items (expectation vs. reality jokes).
- **cheesy-pickups (土味情話)**: Add 廢話文學-style pickup lines (obvious-yet-sincere format). Also add 母親節 crossover ("媽，你就是我人生最強的 buff").

### New Topic Recommendations

1. **負能量職場語錄 / Workplace Sarcasm Quotes** (slug: `workplace-quotes`, category: Lifestyle)
   - Confirmed high-authority coverage on udn.com, popdaily.com.tw, 518.com.tw, yes123.com.tw, womany.net — all have dedicated "職場厭世語錄" articles
   - Dominant tone in 2026: 厭世 (world-weary) + 療癒 (healing through humor) combo — not just complaints, but relatable cynicism that makes people feel seen
   - Verified sample hit formats: "上班領的不是薪水，是精神賠償金"; "工作不會害你，只有人才會"; "我的錢包就像洋蔥，打開它就會想哭"
   - Strong LINE sharing culture among 25–45 demographic; scores well on social platforms during Monday mornings and year-end review seasons
   - SEO targets: 職場語錄, 上班族語錄, 職場厭世, 社畜語錄, 辦公室金句, 工作心聲
   - FunTextHub differentiation: focus on humor + recognition, avoid pure negativity; balance "戳心" with a wry laugh
   - **Recommendation: Create immediately — demand thoroughly confirmed across multiple sources**

2. **勵志語錄 / Motivational Quotes** (slug: `motivational-quotes`, category: Motivation)
   - Multiple high-authority Taiwan sites confirmed still active: arielhsu.tw (101 sentences, 108 sentences articles), projectmanager.com.tw (200 sentences), cyberlink.com/blog, 經理人 (39 curated quotes)
   - Content angles: 追夢 (chasing dreams), 勇氣 (courage), 自我成長 (self-growth), 重新開始 (new beginnings)
   - Seasonal peaks: January (new year), September (back-to-school), year-end reviews — all evergreen anchors
   - FunTextHub differentiator: "輕勵志" only — witty, relatable, non-preachy; target under-30-character sentences
   - SEO targets: 勵志語錄, 正能量語錄, 激勵短句, 座右銘, 每日一句, 心靈短句
   - **Recommendation: Create in parallel with workplace-quotes**

3. **端午節笑話集 / Dragon Boat Festival Jokes** (slug: `holiday-jokes`, category: Humor)
   - Dragon Boat Festival 2026: June 19–21 (Friday–Sunday) — confirmed via TVBS news post
   - Active 端午節 meme content on memes.tw (dedicated tag page), plus 有肉 SUCCULAND already published 75-sentence 端午節賀詞 for 2026
   - Primary joke format: 粽 (zòng) 諧音梗 — "祝你諸事通" → "諸事粽"; wordplay exploiting the phonetics of 粽子
   - Bilingual opportunity: English "dragon boat" puns, "dumpling" jokes, egg puns crossover from Easter content
   - Broader holiday framework: could also serve 中秋節 (Sept 25–27, 2026), 教師節 (Sept 28), 國慶日 (Oct 9–11)
   - SEO targets: 端午節笑話, 端午節梗, 粽子笑話, 端午節祝福語幽默, Dragon Boat Festival jokes
   - **Recommendation: Plan content in late May for June traffic peak; start with 粽 homophone jokes (10–15 items)**

4. **星座語錄 / Zodiac Personality Quotes** (slug: `zodiac-quotes`, category: Social)
   - 2026 is Year of the Fire Horse — Chinese zodiac content has special annual relevance; weekly Chinese horoscope search traffic confirmed active (YourTango data shows ongoing engagement)
   - Western zodiac + personality type hybrid content popular: "牡羊座就是那種…" format consistently shared on IG Taiwan
   - Crossover with I人/E人 slang (see Content Trends below) — zodiac personality labels map directly onto this trending format
   - SEO targets: 星座語錄, 12星座特質, 星座金句, 星座情話, 星座幹話
   - **Recommendation: Develop after workplace-quotes; zodiac is evergreen and not time-pressured**

### Content Trends

- **2026 Top Z-gen Slang (Use in Tags and editorNotes)**:
  - 「朋朋」(friendly buddy term, ~357k Threads/IG mentions) — warm, casual address
  - 「接住」(to emotionally catch/support someone, ~284k mentions) — "接住你的情緒" is the phrase
  - 「I人／E人」(introvert/extrovert, ~267k mentions) — MBTI shorthand now mainstream in Taiwan
  - 「情緒價值」(emotional value — does this interaction give me emotional fulfillment?)
  - 「很躁」(very agitated/restless)
  - 「朋友感」(feeling of genuine friendship/connection)
  - These terms should appear naturally in editorNotes for cheesy-pickups, sweet-quotes, and zodiac-quotes

- **勞動節連假 (May 1–3, 2026)**: Three-day weekend coming up in 19 days. Workplace quotes and 社畜 content will have high search traffic right before and during the holiday. Consider scheduling workplace-quotes launch around late April to capture this wave.

- **端午節 (June 19–21, 2026)**: 68 days away. Recommended content preparation window: late May. 粽 homophone puns are the core format. Research confirms active meme creation culture around this holiday on memes.tw.

- **Global April 2026 Memes (for content inspiration)**:
  - "KitKat Heist" meme (400,000 KitKats stolen in Europe) — absurdist real-life story format; could inspire a cold-joke angle
  - "Nihilistic Penguin" — brand-adopted meme format aligns with 廢話文學 deadpan style already in absurd-wisdom
  - "tfw you didn't agree to this" DiCaprio — reaction format popular globally; 幹話 equivalent would be "誰答應你的"

- **I人/E人 Content Opportunity**: The introvert/extrovert identity slang is highly active. A short-form content angle: "I人的內心OS" jokes and "E人約你出去" situations — fits cold-jokes or a future social-situations topic

### Existing Topic Updates

- **workplace-quotes (pending creation)**: Launch timing matters — target before 勞動節 (May 1) for maximum seasonal relevance. Include a "上班族限定" tag for discoverability.
- **absurd-wisdom (廢話文學)**: Add items using 「接住」 and 「朋友感」 slang angles. E.g.: "如果你接住了所有人的情緒，記得也要留一隻手接住自己的" — sounds profound, is obvious. Fits the format perfectly.
- **sweet-quotes (暖男語錄)**: The 「接住」 slang maps perfectly to romantic context — "I想接住你所有的不安" would resonate with the 接住 trend. Add 1–2 items using this language.
- **cold-jokes (冷笑話)**: Add「I人/E人」joke items. Classic format: "I人的浪漫：傳訊息問你吃飽了嗎，然後在你回覆前已後悔自己主動開口". Tag with 「I人」for discoverability.
- **cheesy-pickups (土味情話)**: The 「朋朋」 term makes an excellent setup for pickup lines: "朋朋，我今天可以叫你男女朋友的朋嗎？" — casual, warm, trendy.

   - SEO targets: 治癒系語錄, 療癒語錄, 暖心短句, 心靈療癒, 治癒金句, healing quotes, 暖心語錄

   - Human Design uses birth time + date + location to generate a "chart" (圖) and assigns one of 5 Types: Generator (生產者), Manifesting Generator (顯示生產者), Projector (投射者), Manifestor (顯示者), Reflector (反映者)

### New Topic Recommendations

1. **大人語錄 / Adulting Quotes** (slug: `adulting-quotes`, category: Lifestyle)
   - DailyView and teamplan.com.tw confirm "初級大人 vs 高級大人" is the biggest 2026 Q1 Threads trend: 39,557 discussion posts from January 1 to April 7 — explosive viral growth from near-zero baseline (only 45 posts in H2 2025)
   - Concept: "高級大人" = someone others defer to for decisions, with authority and experience; "初級大人" = still figuring it out, still being guided by others
   - Highly relatable to FunTextHub's core 20s–40s audience: captures the dissonance of feeling like you're winging adulthood
   - Content angles: "高級大人才懂的事：不解釋，不比較，不委屈"; "初級大人：請假前要看老闆臉色。高級大人：批假前要看月曆顏色"; "以為長大就可以不用補作業，沒想到改名叫做任務追蹤"
   - Cross-format potential: pairs naturally with witty-comebacks and absurd-wisdom; "初級大人/高級大人" format can generate many entries
   - SEO targets: 初級大人, 高級大人, 大人語錄, 長大語錄, 成熟語錄, 大人的世界, adulting quotes, growing up quotes
   - **Recommendation: MEDIUM-HIGH priority. Trend is at peak NOW (Q1 2026 viral wave). Create within 1–2 weeks to capture SEO while search interest is high. Target 10–12 items.**

2. **貓咪語錄 / Cat Quotes** (slug: `cat-quotes`, category: Humor)
   - Multiple 2026 evidence points: memes.tw 貓 tag is actively used; FamilyMart Taiwan Threads account is using cat-format corporate posts ("任何主動貓上班、貓聽話... 都是AI，都是假的啦"); 香蕉貓 (Banana Cat) crying meme was referenced in 2026 央視春晚small-format crossover content
   - Cat meme culture has become mainstream enough for brand Threads accounts to use it — confirms audience breadth beyond niche meme fans
   - Distinct from animal-memes concept: cat-quotes is specifically quote-format content ("貓咪告訴你：我不是在發呆，我是在思考你為什麼那麼奇怪"), not random animal image memes
   - Strong LINE forwarding behavior: cat quotes with human overlay humor ("主子邏輯：我蹬你一腳，是因為你讓我太舒服了") are among the most-forwarded format in Taiwan friend groups
   - SEO targets: 貓咪語錄, 貓語錄, 貓咪金句, 貓迷因, 貓咪搞笑, cat quotes, 貓貓語錄

### Content Trends

- **初級大人/高級大人 Viral Wave (Confirmed Peak)**: teamplan.com.tw 2026 Threads viral guide confirms this is the top Taiwan Threads trend of Q1 2026 (39,557 posts). DailyView published a dedicated analysis with a self-assessment test. The trend has crossed from Threads into news coverage, which historically signals ~2–4 weeks remaining at peak engagement before it normalizes. FunTextHub should act within this window.

### New Topic Recommendations

1. **減肥語錄 / 健身厭世語錄 / Diet & Fitness Quotes** (slug: `diet-quotes` or `fitness-quotes`, category: Lifestyle)
   - UDN article "減肥人生15句哀怨共感語錄" + UBeauty "15句搞笑減肥語錄" both confirm structural search demand for self-deprecating diet humor
   - Format proven viral: "世界上最動聽的3個字，不是『我愛你』，而是『你瘦了』"; "減肥沒有那麼容易，每塊贅肉都有它的脾氣"; "世界上最痛苦的三角戀：我愛食物，脂肪愛我"
   - Year-round demand with two seasonal peaks: 春夏 (May–July, 比基尼季 + 婚禮季) and 年後 (Feb, 過年後減肥) — May launch captures the spring fitness motivation peak directly
   - Differentiator: distinct from healing-quotes (這是自嘲) and motivational-quotes (沒有勵志，是擺爛); the register is 厭世共感 + 食物擺爛幽默
   - Sub-formats: 健身房語錄 (fitness gym humor), 減肥宣言 vs 真實 (intent vs. reality format), 體重計 vs 鏡子 (the scale's lies), 健身教練金句 (trainer-style faux-motivation), 飲食控制廢話 (diet control absurdism)
   - SEO targets: 減肥語錄, 減肥金句, 健身語錄, 減肥幽默, 健身房幽默, 減肥厭世, 體重計語錄, fitness quotes zh-tw
   - **Recommendation: HIGH priority (highest of new candidates this report). Strong content pool, immediate seasonal hook, clear differentiation, high LINE/Threads shareability among 25–45 demographic. Target 12–15 items. Create May (after backlog + 自愛語錄).**

2. **婚禮金句 / 婚禮致詞語錄 / Wedding Speech & Toasts** (slug: `wedding-quotes`, category: Romance)
   - 結婚金句搜尋 confirms strong demand around 春夏婚季 (May–June peak) — Pinkoi "100句結婚金句" + StoryWed 致詞範例 both 2026-active
   - Format proven viral: "婚禮要早上辦。這樣如果搞砸了，也不會浪費整天"; "你終於成功把自己推銷出去了！貨已售出，概不退換"; "愛就像一條電熱毯，但開關掌控在別人手裡"
   - Search intent is high-purpose (people NEED these for actual events) → high time-on-page, low bounce, strong SEO signal
   - Sub-formats: 新郎致詞幽默版, 新娘宣言, 伴郎/伴娘吐槽詞, 紅包賀詞俏皮版, 致父母感謝詞, LINE 群組婚禮祝福
   - Differentiator from sweet-quotes (private love expression) and cheesy-pickups (flirting): wedding-quotes is public-event speech; bilingual register works well for international weddings
   - SEO targets: 婚禮致詞, 結婚金句, 婚禮金句, 新郎致詞, 新娘致詞, 結婚祝福, 婚禮幽默, wedding speech zh-tw, 婚禮紅包賀詞
   - **Recommendation: MEDIUM-HIGH priority. Create May–June. Captures 婚季 traffic. Target 15+ items split across 致詞 / 賀詞 / 吐槽 / 感謝 sub-formats.**

3. **考試語錄 / 學生厭世語錄 / Student Exam Quotes** (slug: `student-quotes` or `exam-quotes`, category: Lifestyle)
   - Dcard 笑話板 + 考試板 + 重考板 confirm constant student-driven joke circulation; "大家期中考要菜菜撈撈嗎" pattern signals 段考/期中考 共感格式 strong
   - Annual cyclical peaks: 學測 (Jan), 段考 (Apr/Nov), 期末 (June/Jan), 指考 (Jul) — 4+ traffic peaks per year vs. typical 1–2 for seasonal topics
   - Distinct audience cohort (high school + university students 16–22) currently underserved by FunTextHub catalog (closest = graduation-quotes which is leaving-school not in-school)
   - Sub-formats: 考前一天語錄, 段考廢話文學, 重考生厭世, 學測倒數金句, 翹課宣言, 大學生熬夜語錄, 不及格自嘲
   - SEO targets: 考試語錄, 學生語錄, 段考語錄, 學測倒數, 考試厭世, 重考語錄, 翹課語錄, 大學生語錄

   - **Recommendation: MEDIUM priority. Create June (segment with graduation-quotes for 畢業 + 期末 dual peak), or hold for July 指考 / Sept 開學 launch. Target 12 items.**

### Content Trends

- **Mother's Day Linguistic Shift Confirmed**: BenQ + Pinkoi + Cyberlink all converge on 2026 母親節 dominant phrasing being **bittersweet-tender** rather than purely celebratory. Top format: "媽媽的碎碎念念，溫暖了我的歲歲年年"; "小時候最想做的事是快快長大，而長大後最希望的事是你慢慢變老"; "你眼中，家是一個地方；媽媽眼中，家是有你在的一段時光". Verify mom-quotes captures this **快快長大 vs. 慢慢變老 對比格式** — it's the single most circulated 2026 母親節 format. ETtoday "10大母親節暖心金句" article still active = ranking proof. **Action: spot-check mom-quotes for this format; if absent, add as urgent priority within next 4 days.**

- **2026 勞動節 全國統一放假 — Final Window**: NOWnews + UDN + Threads @hong.liji + @nownews + @tvbslivenews all confirm 2026 is the historic first year. Threads viral format: "今年起變成勞工無法休息（去年5/1還只有勞工放假，我原本可以找老朋友聚餐旅遊，今年起小孩子也跟著老師學校全都放假）對我來說5/1就跟平常週末一樣，到底是誰搞出這種8" — this is **EXACTLY** the angle workplace-quotes needs. Use this as direct source register (rewrite, don't copy). **Window closes May 1; after May 4 the topic is dead until 2027.**

- **Threads 2026 New Year Quote Format = April Active**: @chicbaby8937 post "願你給出去的柔軟，都能以更好的形狀回到你身邊" + "不急著證明什麼，把心放在舒服的位置" + "留一點力氣給自己，而不是全給別人" — these 2026 自我溫柔語錄 are still circulating in April (4 months after New Year), confirming non-seasonal evergreen status. Pattern: **"願你 + [柔軟動詞] + [回到/接住/陪伴]"** is the dominant 2026 IG/Threads quote frame. Healing-quotes and self-love-quotes (when created) should heavily lean into this exact frame.

- **Diet/Fitness Self-Deprecation = New Niche Confirmed**: UDN 2026 article "減肥人生15句哀怨共感語錄" recently published + matches the broader 2025–2026 厭世共感 trend (廢話文學 → 大人語錄 → 減肥語錄 lineage). The format "[激勵語錄結構] + [擺爛結局]" is a structural template that works across many lifestyle topics. **Apply this template insight to diet-quotes when created.**

- **Persistent Backlog Reality Check**: 16 reports recommending the same three updates without execution = research log has lost actionability. The recommendations are correct (all three trends remain confirmed-active in 2026-04-28 search results: I人/E人 still circulating, 「接住」 still in 2026 New Year quote stream, MBTI/硬控/朋朋 still on Dcard). **Recommend: drop these from "execute" priority and reframe as "if updating these topics for any reason, include these specific items." The persistent restating is generating noise without action.**

4. **自愛語錄 / Self-Love Quotes** (slug: `self-love-quotes`, category: Lifestyle) — **CARRYING FORWARD; longest-deferred carry**

Also surfaces **雙重觀點**: 替老闆抱不平派 ("放太多公司會倒") vs. 勞工發聲派 ("沒有員工哪來老闆") — workplace-quotes can carry both registers. WINDOW CLOSES MAY 4. After that, dead until 2027.

This is the kind of viral that doesn't fit single-quote schema BUT can seed witty-comebacks items: e.g. "別人問你要不要一起吃，就回『我吃一點』，然後吃光" register. **Action: include 1–2 「我吃一點」 derivative items in next witty-comebacks update.**

1. **失戀語錄 / 分手金句 / Breakup & Heartbreak Quotes** (slug: `breakup-quotes`, category: Romance)

   - Format proven viral: 「最好的放下，是不再打擾」「不是每場相遇都有結局，但每場相遇都有意義」「我們都很好，只是時間不湊巧」「失戀的時候有多痛，就意味著你對他的愛有多深」
   - Distinct register from existing romance topics: sweet-quotes = 在愛中的甜蜜, cheesy-pickups = 開始追求, korean-drama-quotes = 戲劇愛情金句; breakup-quotes fills the **離開後的療癒** gap that's currently absent
   - Differentiator from healing-quotes (general 治癒) — breakup-quotes is **specifically post-relationship**, with sub-formats: 釋懷期 (放下), 振作期 (找回自己), 自嘲期 (黑色幽默), 反思期 (時間/緣分), 致前任 (再見不見)
   - Year-round demand: no specific season but consistent search volume; high LINE-share intent ("傳給剛分手的朋友"); IG/Threads quote-card-native format
   - SEO targets: 失戀語錄, 分手金句, 失戀語錄 IG, 心碎語錄, 釋懷語錄, 放下感情 語錄, 失戀療癒, breakup quotes zh-tw

2. **厭世媽媽語錄 / Cynical Mom Quotes** (slug: `cynical-mom-quotes` or merged into `mom-quotes`, category: Lifestyle)
   - PopDaily (3集系列), MomBaby (名畫×厭世媽媽 viral combo), YODEE (10句), 農純鄉blog all confirmed 2026-active

   - **Key strategic question**: separate topic OR sub-feature within mom-quotes? Argument for separate: mom-quotes register is 暖心母親節 (recipient = 媽媽); 厭世媽媽語錄 register is 共感擺爛 (audience = 自己也是媽媽). Different audiences, different LINE share targets (孩子→媽媽 vs. 媽媽→媽媽群). Argument for merged: avoids fragmentation; mom-quotes already exists with established SEO.
   - **Recommendation: MEDIUM-HIGH; create as expansion within mom-quotes** (cheaper, leverages existing SEO equity). Add 5–7 厭世媽媽 items tagged separately for filterable browsing. If post-母親節 traffic data shows the 厭世 register pulls dramatically different audience, spin off in 2026-Q3.
   - Sub-formats: 育兒矛盾語錄 (希望快快長大 vs 不要太快), 媽媽日常崩潰 (沒有自己的時間), 名畫×厭世 對白格式, 媽媽自嘲 (我只是當媽了不是成佛), 孩子怪奇行為解讀 (不出聲必有事), 隊友吐槽 (那個不肯參與的大人)
   - SEO targets: 厭世媽媽語錄, 媽媽崩潰語錄, 媽媽心聲, 育兒厭世, 全職媽媽 共鳴, 媽媽幽默, mom humor zh-tw
   - **Action: include in 母親節 mom-quotes expansion (peak search NOW); evaluate spinoff after 2026-06 traffic review.**

3. **食物笑話 / 諧音梗餐廳店名 / Food Humor & Pun-Name Restaurants** (slug: `food-jokes`, category: Humor) — **CARRYING FORWARD; sharpened with Taiwan 諧音梗店名 文化 angle**
   - 食尚玩家「台南72個諧音哏店名」+ 橘世代「台北6家有梗店名」+ s3.com.tw「20家爆笑諧音梗店名」+ 城市學「諧音建案招牌」all confirm 諧音梗店名 IS a uniquely Taiwanese cultural phenomenon with strong organic content
   - 飲料店命名 confirmed canonical examples: 鶴茶樓 (喝茶囉), 八曜和茶 (爸要喝茶), 可不可 (渴不渴), 龜記 (水果閩南語) — these are stable not transient
   - **Differentiator from cold-jokes**: cold-jokes is 諧音冷笑話 (text-based puns); food-jokes leans into the **店名 + 食物** physical-world humor (現實世界中的諧音梗) which has been underserved
   - Sub-formats: 食物名 諧音梗 (吃飽沒 → 吃寶沒), 飲料店命名爆笑集, 餐廳菜單創意名 (招牌料理諧音), 食物擬人段子 (粽子 vs 月餅 戰爭格式), 名人吃貨段子 (蔡英文「粽所皆知」式), 食物冷知識翻車段子, 大胃王 vs 小鳥胃 對比
   - SEO targets: 食物笑話, 諧音梗 餐廳, 諧音梗 店名, 飲料店 諧音, 美食 笑話, 食物 段子, 食物冷知識, food jokes zh-tw, taiwan pun restaurants
   - **Recommendation: MEDIUM-HIGH (upgraded from MEDIUM). The 諧音梗店名 angle gives food-jokes unique cultural rooting that no other zh-tw food-quote site has captured. Create May–June (端午節 tie-in possible — 粽子 諧音梗 segment can soft-launch the topic ahead of 端午節 traffic). Target 15+ items.**

### Content Trends

- **2026 Q2 NEW Z-Gen Slang Wave Emerging — 泉/要確欸/爛**: s3.com.tw + udn 女子漾 「2026必會網路流行語8條」articles confirm a fresh wave of Taiwanese-Z-gen terms beyond the 2025 朋朋/接住/I人E人 set. **「泉」**: 台語「濺」音轉，形容說話誇大其詞、吹牛不實。**「要確欸」**: 「你要確定欸」簡寫，傻眼/不甘置信時的調侃。**「爛」**: 台語「丟掉」音，表達反感或捨棄。These are 2026-fresh and absent from slang-quotes initial release. **Action: queue Q2 slang-quotes refresh (3–5 new items: 泉, 要確欸, 爛 + any others surfaced) for late-May after slang-quotes hits 30-day organic data.**

- **「初級大人 vs 高級大人」聲量爆炸增長 — 880x YoY**: QuickSeek + dailyview 數據確認 2026 Q1 (Jan–Apr) 討論聲量 **39,557筆 vs 2025下半年僅 45筆** — this is one of the steepest viral-term trajectories observed. 2/17 Threads 貼文「各位初級大人，有遇到什麼要找高級大人的事情嗎」單篇 211.7 萬瀏覽 + 2,000+ 留言. **Action: confirm slang-quotes initial release captured this term; if not, this is the single highest-impact addition.** Also still applies to adulting-quotes per 2026-04-29 high-priority action #4.

- **房地產建商 母親節文案格式 = 高情緒共鳴模板**: 「媽媽不記得母親節，你回家的日子就是過節」— Cyberlink + Pinkoi confirm this 房地產 文案格式 is widely circulated. The **「媽媽不記得X，你Y就是Z」** structural template is reusable. mom-quotes verification: confirm at least 1 item uses this 「不記得 X / Y 就是 Z」 對位格式 — it's the single most LINE-shareable 2026 母親節 phrasing for the 不擅言詞的孩子→媽媽 use case.

- **「Home is wherever you are」雙語版本驗證活躍**: BenQ + Pinkoi 2026 母親節 articles consistently surface this English-zh bilingual phrasing pair: 「有妳的地方，就是我最安心的家」/「Home is wherever you are」. **Action: verify sweet-quotes Mother's Day items have at least 1 fully bilingual-resonant pair (zh-tw + en that work as standalone quotes in their own languages, not literal translations) — this is FunTextHub's structural advantage over zh-only competitors and should be deliberately leveraged.**

- **2026 全球 meme 趨勢 — 「real over perfect」 + AI hyperreal**: napoleoncat + brobible + ramd.am 2026-04 confirm dominant global trend = unpolished/authentic content (dad jokes resurgence, meme shirts, "can you see me" relatability audio) + AI hyperreal videos blurring reality/parody line. **Implication for FunTextHub**: positioning as **rewritten authentic-feeling fun text** (not AI-slop, not perfectly-polished) directly aligns with this trend. The rewrite-don't-copy editorial discipline IS the brand moat. No specific content action — confirms strategic direction.

- **台南/台北 諧音梗店名 文化 = 結構性內容資產**: 食尚玩家報導台南72家、橘世代台北6家、城市學論述 confirm 諧音梗店名 是台灣獨特城市現象，每年新案不斷 (餐飲業 + 自助洗衣 + 美容業均加入). 吳彥祖回應「吾燕煮鍋燒」事件示範 viral momentum 可外溢國際. **This validates upgrading food-jokes priority** (recommendation #3 above).

- **失戀語錄 listicle 飽和度 = 強需求訊號**: PopLady 22句 / GirlStyle 15句 / 漫漫日和 / Ariel Hsu 88句 / vocus 10句 / yoki 20句 / Bella 20句 / chatartpro 100句 — 8+ articles all currently ranking. listicle 飽和度高 = 搜尋意圖強 = SEO進入機會仍存在 (long-tail terms 釋懷語錄, 放下感情 語錄, 心碎語錄 等仍有空隙). Validates breakup-quotes recommendation #1.

### New Topic Recommendations

1. **服務業心聲語錄 / Service-Industry Voice Quotes** (slug: `service-quotes`, category: Lifestyle) — **NEW FROM 2026-05-04 viral surfacing**
   - **2026-04-29 新北藍38 公車司機事件**: 司機與乘客爭執後伏在方向盤痛哭「為什麼要欺負司機」, 影片 Threads 流傳 → 4/30 各大媒體 (聯合, 中時, 自由, 星島) + **CNN 全球放送** → 雙北交通局長公開回應. 罕見的 service-industry 情緒崩潰 case 引爆全民共感.
   - **共感範圍遠超公車**: udn 整理「乘車規範」, 各大平台延伸到 餐飲店員 / 客服 / 護理 / 保全 / 便利商店 / 外送員 — 所有 frontline service 行業 都在 Threads/Dcard 集體 貼 共感故事. 「最多笑容、最少尊重」結構性議題.
   - **Differentiator vs workplace-quotes**: workplace-quotes 主軸 = 內勤/上班族 (薪水, 加班, 老闆, 同事). service-quotes 主軸 = 對客戶/民眾 直接 frontline (奧客, 委屈, 笑著吞下情緒, 制服變盔甲). 不同 audience (服務業勞工 ≠ 辦公室 OL), 不同 LINE 分享流通群 (服務業 LINE 群 vs 上班族群).
   - Sub-formats: 奧客語錄 (不可思議的客人發言), 制服底下語錄 (笑著上班崩潰下班), 服務業金句 (「客人不是上帝, 客人是隔壁桌也在等的人」), 行業互助 (公車司機, 餐廳, 便利商店 互相打氣), 工時/薪資對照 厭世 (「服務貴賓的薪水不貴」).
   - SEO targets: 服務業語錄, 服務業 心聲, 奧客語錄, 客服語錄, 公車司機語錄, 服務業 厭世, 服務業 委屈, frontline worker quotes zh-tw
   - **Recommendation: NEW HIGH urgency. 2026-04-29 事件 still trending; topic creation within 1–2 weeks captures discovery wave + builds evergreen authority for recurring service-industry virality. Target 12–15 items balanced across 5 sub-formats. CNN coverage = international SEO halo for en version.**

### New Topic Recommendations

1. **懷舊語錄 / Nostalgia Quotes — 「2026 is the new 2016」系列** (slug: NEW SUB-FORMAT candidate within `motivational-quotes` or `healing-quotes`; OR new topic `nostalgia-quotes` if multi-decade scope, category: Lifestyle) — **NEW 2026-05-05 viral surfacing**
   - **2026 viral trend**: 「2026 is the new 2016」歐美社群 集體懷舊 (TrueFuture / KnowYourMeme / Wikipedia 已收錄為 dedicated meme entry); ELLE Taiwan Threads 貼文 (DTNrOUAE63r) 4/29 同步 amplification → 台灣 IG/Threads 開始 跟進「2016 我在做什麼」+「演算法前的網路」+「Pokémon Go / dabbing / fidget spinner」十年回望 wave.
   - **核心情緒結構**: 不是單純懷舊, 是「revisionism」(revisionist nostalgia) — 對「演算法前 / AI 前 / 政治正確前 / COVID 前」的「最後純真年代」的集體投射. 觸發 millennial (28–38) + 早期 Z-gen (24–28) audience 同時共鳴.
   - **Differentiator vs. healing-quotes**: healing 是「現在/未來」溫柔陪伴; nostalgia 是「過去/失去」的 共感再敘事. 兩者 register 不同, 不衝突.
   - **Differentiator vs. motivational-quotes**: motivational 是「向前」, nostalgia 是「回望」. 但兩者可在「從過去汲取勇氣」處 overlap.
   - Sub-formats 可開發: 「2016 vs 2026」對照格式 (網路文化, 流行音樂, 社群平台)、十年回望短句、「那年的你不知道」感性、「謝謝那個時代的我」自愛接合.
   - SEO targets: 懷舊語錄, 10年回望, 那年我們, 2016 vs 2026, throwback 語錄, nostalgia quotes
   - **Recommendation: NEW MEDIUM-HIGH urgency. 兩條路徑可選 — (A) 作為 motivational-quotes 或 healing-quotes 的 NEW sub-format (3–5 items, 7 天內) 試水; (B) 若 7–14 天內 ELLE / 風傳媒 / Threads 持續加溫, 升級成獨立 `nostalgia-quotes` topic. 先走 A 路徑.**

2. **「2016 vs 2026」十年對照格式** (sub-format candidate within `slang-quotes`, `adulting-quotes`, OR `motivational-quotes`, NOT new topic) — **DERIVATIVE of #1 above**
   - **獨立列為 sub-format 因 register 完全不同**: 「2016 vs 2026」是結構化對照 (「2016 的我：X / 2026 的我：Y」), 而 #1 nostalgia 是抒情敘事. 對照格式 viral potential 更高 (Threads 短貼文友善).
   - 經典結構候選: 「2016 的我：在 IG 發出去夜店的照片. 2026 的我：在 Threads 發我又取消聚會了」/「2016 的我：fidget spinner. 2026 的我：fidget with my anxiety」/「2016 的我：相信網紅. 2026 的我：相信演算法決定我相信誰」.
   - **Recommendation: MEDIUM. 1–2 items 試播於 adulting-quotes (因初級/高級大人對照已有對照基底), 觀察 7 天 organic.**

3. **寵物離世語錄 / Pet Loss Quotes** (slug: NEW potential — `pet-memorial-quotes` OR sub-format within `cat-quotes` + `dog-quotes`, category: Lifestyle) — **NEW from today's pet research**
   - **Search results 顯示 結構化需求**: hk01 + skypost + multiple HK 媒體 持續 surface「面對喪寵的人有些話不能說」「醫生教放下動作」articles → 這是高搜尋量 evergreen niche, 不限季節.
   - 台灣 寵物擬人化文化 持續強化 (per 2026 cat-quotes / dog-quotes 既有 audience), 「彩虹橋」「毛孩」community 對 高品質 mourning 內容 需求 持續.
   - **Differentiator vs. breakup-quotes**: 失戀是 對人; 寵物離世是 對毛孩. 不同 audience, 不同 LINE 分享 群 (寵物社團 vs 戀愛 PTT/Dcard).
   - Sub-formats: 告別期 (彩虹橋常見比喻), 思念期 (日常觸景生情), 自責期 (「如果那天我...」), 安慰他人 (「別說『再養一隻就好了』」), 撫慰格式 (「你只是先去睡了」).
   - SEO targets: 寵物離世, 毛孩離開, 彩虹橋, pet loss quotes zh-tw, 失寵 安慰
   - **Recommendation: MEDIUM. 30–45 天觀察期 — 不立即建立 topic, 但記錄為 Q3 (8–9月) 候選. 若 cat-quotes / dog-quotes 7天 organic 上 spot 任一 mourning-adjacent 表現, 升級為 HIGH.**

### Content Trends

- **「朋朋」(356,929 筆) + 「接住」(284,309 筆) + 「I人/E人」(266,587 筆) = 2026-Q1 Threads 三大 聲量冠軍流行語**: dailyview 33240 + bnext 80853 + Look Pretty 25872 + quickseek 609 全部 confirm. 這三個詞 在 funtexthub slang-quotes 中的 verification status 是 **2026-05-05 最大未驗證盲點** — 三個詞合計 90 萬+ 月聲量, 若 slang-quotes 漏 任一個 = 失 SEO 主流通路. **CRITICAL: 今天必須 audit slang-quotes 是否涵蓋這三詞**, 缺則 立即補 (各 1–2 items).

- **「朋朋」用法精細化**: 不是「朋友」的縮寫, 而是「網路上認識、沒見過面但很常聊」的中度親密互動關係 (Threads 原生詞). 與「家人」「兄弟」「閨蜜」屬於不同 register. 編寫時須避免簡化為「朋友」.

- **「接住」結構化用法**: 已固定為「情緒接住」(emotional catch) — 「你願意接住我」「我來接住你」. 多在 emo / 抒情 貼文出現, 與 healing-quotes 「願你 + 柔軟動詞」frame 同源. healing-quotes 應有 ≥1 item 直接使用「接住」一詞.

- **「I人/E人」沉澱為日常自介開場詞**: MBTI 標籤 已從「人格分析」轉為「對話加速器」. 幾乎 取代「我比較內向/外向」. slang-quotes 條目應 reflect 此 shift — 「I人」不必解釋 MBTI, 直接視為 communication shortcut.

- **「2026 is the new 2016」十年集體懷舊 wave** (新增): KnowYourMeme + Wikipedia + ELLE Taiwan + The Concordian + lamomoneon.com 多源 confirm. 核心觸發點 = 「演算法前 + AI 前 + COVID 前」三重失樂園投射. **這是 2026-Q2 最大新興 emotional 集體共鳴** — 與既有 healing/motivational 內容互補, 可開發為 register sub-format (3–5 items 試水).

- **「厭世上班族 AI 頭像」Threads 趨勢** (per bnext 83586): ChatGPT-4o 生成 cartoon 厭世 office worker 頭像, prompt 在 Threads 流通. **意義: 「厭世」已從文字 register 擴大到視覺 self-identity**. workplace-quotes 既有「精神賠償金/薪水像月經」metaphor 仍主流, 但可加入「厭世自我宣告」格式 (「我的頭像就是我每天的心情報告」).

- **報稅季「找高級大人」自然 second wave (5月持續)**: yahoo 新聞「手機報稅少1步驟恐少省3萬」近 80 萬 view + 各大媒體 4/30–5/4 連續報稅攻略稿 → 5月 = 「初級大人 自我認同」全年 第二高峰 (僅次於 1–2月 過年). **adulting-quotes 對照格式 5/8 deadline 不能再延 — 失去 5月 = 失今年 70%+ 該 register 流量機會.**

- **公車司機事件 國際 SEO halo 持續發酵**: udn 4 篇 + ETtoday + 三立 + teepr + setn 持續 long-tail 文章 5/1–5/4 仍在 publish. service-quotes 已 0–1 天 live = 進入 SEO 採集週期 高峰 — 主動驗證 5 sub-formats 是否有對應 公車司機 事件 共感 item (不需直接提事件名, 但 phrasings 應 reflect「制服底下的眼淚」「最多笑容最少尊重」核心情緒).

- **五月天 5/15–17 台北大巨蛋 演唱會 + 6/27–7/12 8場 連唱 = 5–7月 青春/告別 emotional content 流量加溫**: 五月天 內容 連動 graduation-quotes (青春告別) + sweet-quotes (情歌情境) + healing-quotes (「諾亞方舟」「如果我們不曾相遇」式 治癒). graduation-quotes 4 NEW 2026 phrasings 補完後, 若可加入「散場後仍記得旋律」/「最後一首歌唱完之後」音樂×畢業 register 1–2 items, 可吃 5月中 跨 fan 群 traffic.

- **wedding-quotes 競爭格局穩定**: pinkoi 2207 + Diamond Shiraishi + storywed 2 篇 + theaisle + chatartpro + cutefigurehk 多源 high DA 競爭已成熟; FunTextHub 進場差異化路線確認 = 「真誠 + 個人化 + 雙語」+「致詞段落結構化」(開場/對另一半/感謝/結尾 各成 quote-card). 5月 母親節 主場期 不創 wedding-quotes — 6月端午後再啟動.

- **「2016 vs 2026」對照格式 = nostalgia × adulting 兩 audience 跨界 sweet spot**: 同時觸發「我老了」(nostalgia) + 「我還沒長大」(adulting 初級大人 register). 1–2 items 試播 即可 spot 兩 audience 重疊度.

### New Topic Recommendations

1. **桃園機場檢疫犬諧音梗 衍生 food-jokes 加碼 sub-format** (sub-format within `food-jokes`, NOT new topic) — **NEW 2026-05-05 viral surfacing**
   - **2026-05-05 Taipei Times 報導 (4-2003856784)**: 桃園國際機場 動植物防檢疫局 推出 一系列 偵檢犬 海報 — 配上「諧音梗 警示語」(beagle 表情包 + 申報提醒). 帖文 ~80 萬瀏覽 (TT confirmed); 台/日網友 互相 quote-share 討論. 「台灣人對諧音梗的偏愛」再度成為 cross-cultural 社群話題.
   - **意義 = 2026-Q2 第二波「諧音梗 cultural moment」** (繼 2024 台南 71 家店名 + 2025 田馥甄玉琴顧粽 之後). food-jokes 上線時機點 巧合捕捉此 wave.
   - Sub-format 候選: 「機場/海關 諧音梗」(非食物但同 register, food-jokes 可彈性收 1–2 items 試水), 或將「檢疫犬警語」reframe 成「狗狗也會諧音梗」的食物 cross-over (狗狗代言食物店招).
   - **Recommendation: MEDIUM (food-jokes 既已上線, 純 sub-format expansion). 1–2 items 試水, 7 天 organic 觀察. 不另開 topic.**

2. **「2026 開年熱梗結構改變」=「句式化 / 評論區化」 — content 編寫 frame 全面 shift** (sub-format candidate within `slang-quotes`, `adulting-quotes`, NOT new topic) — **NEW 2026-05-06 trend insight from 悟空教育 + Lingoace 多源 confirmed**
   - **2026 中文網路梗的核心結構轉變** (per Lingoace + 悟空教育 5/5 同步報導): **以前 viral = 單一詞 (e.g.「破防」「絕絕子」), 2026 viral = 整句句式** (e.g.「注意看，這個男人太狠了」「甘阿捏」「我不裝了我攤牌了」). Threads 的「演算法 + 短文 + 評論區化」推 此 shift 至主流.
   - **意義: funtexthub 的 quote/語錄 內容 已 inherently 是「句式」, 此 shift 對 funtexthub 是順風**. slang-quotes 既有「我吃一點」「破防」單詞 register 應 補入「整句 viral 句式」 register — 「注意看, 這個 X 太狠了」 + 「我不裝了我攤牌了」 + 「甘阿捏」(台灣龍捲風 復古回潮).
   - **新 viral 句式 confirmed**: 「注意看，這個男人太狠了」(中國劇情解說 開場 → 台灣社群 反向 借用), 「甘阿捏」(本土劇 復古回潮), 「我不裝了我攤牌了」.
   - SEO targets: 句式 流行語, 注意看這個男人太狠了, 甘阿捏 梗
   - **Recommendation: MEDIUM-HIGH urgency. slang-quotes 加入「句式 viral」sub-format 3–5 items (2 週內), 補入 2026 結構性 trend shift.** 對 LINE 群分享流通有絕對助益 (整句 ≥ 單詞 share-friendly).

3. **「Threads AI 趨勢摘要」台灣上線 (2026-05-05)— 平台層級 meta shift** (NOT a topic recommendation, but a platform-level signal affecting 所有 topics' SEO strategy) — **NEW 2026-05-05 platform announcement**
   - **TechBriefly 5/5 報導**: Threads AI Trend Summaries 擴展到 台灣 / 越南 / 日本 / 巴西. 此功能 = AI 自動匯整 Threads 平台上 即時話題 + 推送給 用戶. 對 funtexthub 意義: **若 funtexthub 內容 在 Threads 被 quote-share, 將更容易被 AI 摘要 surface = 平台級 SEO 加分**.
   - **可採取的 action**: 持續確保每個 quote 都 Threads-friendly (≤ 280 字, 整句完整, 不依賴 上下文). editorNote 中可加入「適合 Threads 短貼分享」標註 (內部 reference, 非 user-facing).
   - **Recommendation: NO 直接 topic 動作; 但 next 幾個 topic 創建時 (`wedding-quotes`, `food-jokes` expansion) 編寫時應 actively Threads-optimize 句式長度與情緒密度.**

### Content Trends

- **「2026 開年熱梗 句式化 / 評論區化」結構性 shift = 2026 全年 content trend 主軸** (per Lingoace + 悟空教育 雙源 confirmed): 「破防」「絕絕子」單詞 register 仍存活但 momentum 下降; 「注意看, 這個男人太狠了」「甘阿捏」「我不裝了我攤牌了」整句 register 上升. funtexthub 既有 sweet-quotes / healing-quotes / motivational-quotes 「整句完整」設定 = inherent 順風. slang-quotes 是唯一 「單詞」register 為主的 topic — 應 補入 整句 sub-format 補位.

- **「2026 is the new 2016」十年集體懷舊 wave 持續加溫 (Wikipedia + KnowYourMeme dedicated entry confirmed)**: 該 entry 已收錄至 Wikipedia 主文 (en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2026_is_the_new_2016) — 從「短期 viral」升級為「文化條目」. 此 wave 在 5/4–5/6 internet 持續累積 (KnowYourMeme + Instagram + Threads 多平台同步). **5/5 推薦 (#9 nostalgia × healing/motivational 1–2 items 試水) 升級 status: 仍 MEDIUM, 但 Wikipedia entry 確認 = 此 wave 至少 持續到 Q3, 可耐心觀察 7 天 organic 後再決定升級**.

- **桃園機場諧音梗檢疫犬海報 80萬 view (2026-05-05)** = Taipei Times + cross-Twitter Japan 互動報導: 「諧音梗」在 2026-Q2 仍是 台灣 viral 文化 主動脈. food-jokes (5/4–5/5 上線) 上線時機絕對精準. 觀察 7 天 organic 是否帶起 cross-platform pickup.

- **「朋朋」(356K) / 「接住」(284K) / 「I人E人」(266K) 三大冠軍 + 「觸」「觸爛」「觸爆」 + 「卡皮巴拉」+ 「尊嘟假嘟」+ 「已購買小孩愛吃」**: 5/6 多源 (quickseek 609 + bnext 80853 + Look Pretty 25872 + Yahoo Lifestyle udn 9281226) 持續 confirmed. **「卡皮巴拉」= 「情緒穩定 / 呆萌 / 讓人放鬆」核心定位** (per Lingoace 5/5 補釋), slang-quotes 條目 應 reflect 此 emotional register, 不只是「水豚」翻譯.

### New Topic Recommendations

   - **5/7 入夜首波鋒面 + 13縣市大雨特報 push notif** (自由時報今早) + 「梅雨季 5月中下旬–6月上旬」(公視 805737 + 自由 5389393 + 風傳媒 11126919) → 30 天 window 已開. 梅雨 是 evergreen-seasonal trigger (每年 5–6月) — register 開發後 可 reuse 2027/2028.
   - 結構候選: 「衣服晾不乾, 連我都快發霉」 / 「上班通勤被擠濕了三次, 老闆只在乎報表沒水印」 / 「梅雨像我加班 — 連著下七天」 / 「公車上有鹹魚味, 但其實是我」 / 「梅雨季的辦公室冷氣是冰櫃, 我是裡面那條沒醒的鮭魚」.
   - **Differentiator vs. 現有 workplace-quotes**: 既有 register 偏「精神賠償金 / 薪水像月經 / 厭世 AI 頭像」(全年 evergreen). 「梅雨」 specific to 5–6月 weather — 不衝突, 是 seasonal 補位.
   - SEO targets: 梅雨 厭世, 上班 下雨, 通勤 大雨, 梅雨季 心情, 雨天 上班族
   - **Recommendation: NEW MEDIUM-HIGH urgency, 7-DAY WINDOW (5/7–5/14).** workplace-quotes 加 3–5 items `rainy-season` register. 因 30 天 window 從今天起算, 且 5/7 大雨特報 push notif 已 viral peak — 越早上 越吃 SEO. 5/14 之後 traffic 衰減 但仍可 serve 整個梅雨季.

2. **「母親節最後 72 小時」 emotional triple — 訂不到位 / 媽媽不缺什麼 / 不要送廚具」 sub-format / opportunistic items within `mom-quotes` + `sweet-quotes`** (NOT new topic) — **NEW 2026-05-07 day-of register surfaced**
   - **5/7 多源 confirm**: Threads (@globalfoodelicious DXiXBaCkyyd) + udn 9484577 + Trip.com + RosyArts + Pinkoi + Beauty321 71645 同步 surface「最後一刻訂位崩潰」「其實我什麼都不缺」「不要送不實用廚具」「她需要做回女孩, 不是優化勞動」 三 register.
   - **意義: 母親節 5/10 day-of register 是 5/7-5/10 集體 viral 情緒** — funtexthub mom-quotes / sweet-quotes 既有 5/6 封盤 偏「感恩 / 家×時光 / 慢慢變老」 (歌頌 register), 但「day-of 焦慮」(訂不到位 / 送禮焦慮 / 不要再優化我的勞動) 是 NEW 反差 register — 與「歌頌」並存.
   - 結構候選 (rephrase, 不 copy): 「媽說她什麼都不缺, 但她不缺的時候笑得最尷尬」 / 「訂不到位的母親節, 是我們欠媽媽的第二次成績單」 / 「請不要送她廚具, 她需要的是讓人替她洗碗的那個下午」 / 「媽媽今天不想當媽媽, 她想當她自己 — 哪怕只有兩小時」.
   - **Differentiator vs. 既有「家×時光」frame**: 「家×時光」是 over-arching 抒情; 「day-of 焦慮 / 反差」是 戰術級 specific moment (餐廳訂位 / 廚具送禮 / 「我什麼都不缺」). 戰術級 register 在 LINE 群分享時 比 抒情 更高 share-rate.
   - SEO targets: 母親節 訂不到, 母親節 不要送, 媽媽 什麼都不缺, 母親節 焦慮, 媽媽不想當媽媽
   - **Recommendation: NEW MEDIUM-HIGH urgency. 3 DAYS WINDOW (5/7–5/10) — 機會窗口極短.** 但 5/6 已大封盤 + 今日 5/7 是 day-of register surfacing 第一天 → 兩條路徑可選: (A) 不再開封 mom-quotes / sweet-quotes, 純 observe 7天, 把「day-of 反差」放進 evergreen Q4 母親節 backlog; (B) 若 編輯方願意 開 minor patch, 各 topic +1 item 試水 (僅當有 5/8–5/9 編輯預定). **Default = (A) — 5/6 封盤決策不打破; 把 register 記入 2027 母親節 backlog 即可**.

### Content Trends

   - **5/8 reverify**: 115 學測 已於 2026/01/17-19 結束, 指考 (分科測驗) 排定 **2026/07/11-12** = 64 days from today. 5/7 推薦 #13 「6 月或 7月」 timing **修正為 6月底-7月初啟動最佳** (T-7 to T-14 days = 6/27-7/4 上線 = 學生焦慮高峰前) → 啟動時間從「June or July」 sharpen 為 「late June」.
   - **意義**: 學測族流量已過 (1月主場), **2026/7/11-12 分科測驗 是 7月唯一 大流量 文教 hook**. funtexthub 既有 graduation-quotes 處理 5月畢業 / 7月大學入學, 但 「考試焦慮 / 答錯題 / 應屆 vs 重考 / 夜讀」 frame 是 graduation-quotes 不直接覆蓋 的 niche.
   - 結構候選: 「我比答案紙更想交卷」/「夜讀 三千頁, 進入考場 三秒鐘」/「應屆生 vs 重考生 vs 在重考的應屆生」 對照 / 「答錯也沒關係, 反正人生很多題本來就沒答案」/「考完那一刻, 比放榜還像放榜」.
   - SEO targets: 考試 焦慮, 指考 心情, 分科測驗 語錄, 學測 心得, 夜讀 廢文.
   - **Recommendation: PROMOTE Q3 → late June (T-2 weeks before 7/11 指考)**. 6月底 啟動, 7月初 上線, 5+ items, 2026 全年 第二大 文教 流量 hook.

3. **`insomnia-quotes` / 失眠語錄 — NEW Q3 候選 (低-中優先級)**
   - **5/8 多源**: udn 9488575「越想睡越睡不著 醫師揭反直覺助眠法」+ vocus 68552a49「Sunday Night Blues」+ 維力骨科 「收假症候群 失眠」 + 康健 「焦慮 上班族 心悸」+ 全球新興 心理健康 baseline. 「失眠 = 太想睡」「Sunday night blues」「收假症候群」三 register 是 evergreen 心理 主題.
   - **意義 vs. healing-quotes / self-love-quotes**: healing-quotes 是「治癒/陪伴」 register; self-love-quotes 是「自我接納」 register; **「失眠」 是 niche behavioral state (specific 凌晨 3 點 / 滑手機 / 數羊 / 周日晚焦慮) — 與 既有 兩 topic 不衝突**, 是 evergreen low-competition niche.
   - 結構候選: 「凌晨三點的我 比凌晨三點的世界 更清醒」/「我的羊群 已經數到改名叫『綿羊小華』」/「失眠不是我睡不著, 是我太想要它」/「周日晚上的恐懼 比周一早上 真實一千倍」/「滑手機 是 失眠的儀式, 不是 原因」.
   - SEO targets: 失眠 語錄, 凌晨 三點, 數羊 廢文, 周日 焦慮, sunday night blues.
   - **Recommendation: NEW Q3 候選 (8-9月 評估)** — 不立即. healing-quotes / self-love-quotes Q2 organic 表現 觀察後決定 是否 開. 若 self-love-quotes 5/13 monitor 結束後 traffic OK, **insomnia-quotes 可以 8月 試水, evergreen low-competition niche**.

- **梅雨 day-2 (5/8) 持續加溫**: 5/7 入夜首波鋒面 + 5/8 全台陰雨 + 5月中下旬 梅雨主場期. workplace-quotes 「梅雨厭世」 7-day window (5/7-5/14) day-2/7. 5/8 編輯方若 touch workplace-quotes, 「衣服晾不乾」/「公車鹹魚味」/「雨天加班」 frame 3-5 items priority. healing-quotes 「願你撐傘的時候, 也有人在傘下接住你」 frame 1-2 items 跨 「梅雨 + 接住 + 停止內耗」三趨勢.

1. **slang-quotes 「留友看」 Threads 平台 metagame register — NEW 5/9 register expansion (NOT NEW TOPIC)**

   - **意義 vs. slang-quotes 既有 register**: slang-quotes 39 items 既有 ven / 朋朋 / 接住 / I人E人 / 觸 / 卡皮巴拉 / 尊嘟假嘟 / 注意看這個男人太狠了 / 我不裝了我攤牌了 / 甘阿捏 / 要確欸 / 躁 / 破防 / 初級高級大人 等. **「留友看」 是 slang-quotes 既有 register 缺口**: 唯一 「平台 metagame 動詞」 (其他都是 情緒/狀態/句式), 是 Threads-native register, 5/20 deadline 編寫 priority register +1 列入.
   - SEO targets: 留友看, threads 流行語, threads 用語, 留言 友看, 平台梗.
   - **Recommendation: slang-quotes 5/20 deadline (T-11) 編寫時 priority register +1, 「留友看」 1-2 items 在地化 (e.g.「這則 留友看 / 留你的人 看 / 你不留 我幫你留 / 留友看 = 友 都看不到 因為演算法不給力」 register).** **NOT NEW TOPIC**.
